     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Media">
       Media
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Media">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <table class="metadata plainlinks ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">
      <tr>
       <td class="mbox-image">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg">
         <img alt="[icon]" data-file-height="31" data-file-width="44" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/>
        </a>
       </td>
       <td class="mbox-text">
        <span class="mbox-text-span">
         This section requires
         <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit">
          expansion
         </a>
         .
         <small>
          <i>
           (October 2012)
          </i>
         </small>
        </span>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </table>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:TsingtauerNeuesteNachrichten1Nov1904.png">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="344" data-file-width="856" height="88" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/TsingtauerNeuesteNachrichten1Nov1904.png/220px-TsingtauerNeuesteNachrichten1Nov1904.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/TsingtauerNeuesteNachrichten1Nov1904.png/330px-TsingtauerNeuesteNachrichten1Nov1904.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/TsingtauerNeuesteNachrichten1Nov1904.png/440px-TsingtauerNeuesteNachrichten1Nov1904.png 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:TsingtauerNeuesteNachrichten1Nov1904.png" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Tsingtauer_Neueste_Nachrichten" title="Tsingtauer Neueste Nachrichten">
          Tsingtauer Neueste Nachrichten
         </a>
        </i>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Qingdao previously had a large German community and a German garrison, so three German newspapers operated in Qingdao.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Walravens90_40-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Walravens90-40">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        40
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      German papers included
      <i>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Deutsch-Asiatische_Warte&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Deutsch-Asiatische Warte (page does not exist)">
        Deutsch-Asiatische Warte
       </a>
      </i>
      (T: , S: , P:
      <i>
       Tidng Gjn Jin
      </i>
      ;
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Walravens91_41-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Walravens91-41">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        41
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      weekly newspaper published until 1906, included
      <i>
       Die Welt des Ostens, Altes und Neues aus Asiens drei Kaiserreichen
      </i>
      , a cultural supplement),
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Walravens90_40-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Walravens90-40">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        40
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      the
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Tsingtauer_Neueste_Nachrichten" title="Tsingtauer Neueste Nachrichten">
        Tsingtauer Neueste Nachrichten
       </a>
      </i>
      and the
      <i>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Kiautschou_Post&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Kiautschou Post (page does not exist)">
        Kiautschou Post
       </a>
      </i>
      (a daily paper published from 1908 to 1912, referring to the
      <a href="/wiki/Kiautschou_Bay_concession" title="Kiautschou Bay concession">
       Kiautschou (Jiaozhou) Bay concession
      </a>
      ). German publishing in Qingdao ended after
      <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">
       World War I
      </a>
      and the beginning of the Japanese administration.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Walravens91_41-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Walravens91-41">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        41
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      A 1912 publication of the
      <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Commerce" title="United States Department of Commerce">
       United States Department of Commerce
      </a>
      ,
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bureau_of_Foreign_and_Domestic_Commerce" title="Bureau of Foreign and Domestic Commerce">
       Bureau of Foreign and Domestic Commerce
      </a>
      said that the
      <i>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Tageblatt_f%C3%BCr_Nordchina&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Tageblatt fr Nordchina (page does not exist)">
        Tageblatt fr Nordchina
       </a>
      </i>
      of
      <a href="/wiki/Tianjin" title="Tianjin">
       Tianjin
      </a>
      was read in Qingdao, and that major newspapers from
      <a href="/wiki/Shanghai" title="Shanghai">
       Shanghai
      </a>
      were also read in Qingdao.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">
       <a href="#cite_note-42">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        42
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Tourism">
       Tourism
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Tourism">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Qingdao attracts many tourists due to its seaside setting and temperate weather. Parks, beaches, sculpture and unique German and modern architecture line the shore. The central tourist information is called
      <b>
       Qingdao Information Centre for International Visitors
      </b>
      and located on Mid-Hong Kong Road ( pinyin: Xinggng Zhngl).
     </p>
     <p>
      Qingdao's major attractions include:
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Western_part_of_Shinan_district_.28.E5.B8.82.E5.8D.97.E5.8C.BA.E8.A5.BF.E9.83.A8.29">
       Western part of Shinan district ()
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Western part of Shinan district ()">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Zhan_Qiao" title="Zhan Qiao">
        Zhan Qiao (Pier, )
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       Little Qingdao Isle ()
      </li>
      <li>
       Tian Hou Temple (), Qingdao Folk Museum
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Ba_Da_Guan" title="Ba Da Guan">
        Ba Da Guan (Eight Great Passes, )
       </a>
       , the older area of town with some surviving German and Japanese architecture.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Lu_Xun_Park_(Qingdao)" title="Lu Xun Park (Qingdao)">
        Lu Xun Park
       </a>
       , named after
       <a href="/wiki/Lu_Xun" title="Lu Xun">
        Lu Xun
       </a>
       (), modern Chinese writer and critic, who lived and taught in the 1930s.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.qdzsgy.com/" rel="nofollow">
        Zhongshan Park
       </a>
       , named after the style name 'Zhongshan' of
       <a href="/wiki/Sun_Yat-sen" title="Sun Yat-sen">
        Sun Yat-sen
       </a>
       (), a famous modern Chinese politician.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Xiao_Yu_Shan" title="Xiao Yu Shan">
        Xiao Yu Shan (Little Fish Hill, )
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.qdzwy.com/" rel="nofollow">
        Qingdao Botanical Garden
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.qdzoo.net/" rel="nofollow">
        Qingdao Zoological Garden
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       The twin-spired
       <a href="/wiki/St._Michael%27s_Cathedral,_Qingdao" title="St. Michael's Cathedral, Qingdao">
        St. Michael's Cathedral
       </a>
       (), one piece of the famous
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Neo-romanesque" title="Neo-romanesque">
        Neo-romanesque
       </a>
       architecture in Qingdao, designed by German architect Alfred Frbel, completed in 1934.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Huashi_Villa&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Huashi Villa (page does not exist)">
        Huashi Villa
       </a>
       (), a mansion originally built for a Russian aristocrat
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_Aquarium" title="Qingdao Aquarium">
        Qingdao Aquarium
       </a>
      </li>

      <span class="mw-headline" id="Eastern_part_of_Shinan_district_.28.E5.B8.82.E5.8D.97.E5.8C.BA.E4.B8.9C.E9.83.A8.29">
       Eastern part of Shinan district ()
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>

       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>

        May Fourth Square
       </a>
       Coastal plaza with the Wind of May sculpture
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Music_Square&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Music Square (page does not exist)">
        Music Square
       </a>
       , famous for
       <b>
        the Sail of Music
       </b>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao_Seaside_Sightseeing_Path&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Qingdao Seaside Sightseeing Path (page does not exist)">
        Qingdao Seaside Sightseeing Path
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao_International_Beer_town&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Qingdao International Beer town (page does not exist)">
        Qingdao International Beer town
       </a>
       , the primary site of the annual
       <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_International_Beer_Festival" title="Qingdao International Beer Festival">
        Qingdao International Beer Festival
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Tsingtao_Brewery" title="Tsingtao Brewery">
        Tsingtao Brewery
       </a>
       , originally founded by Germans and the most exported beer from China.
      </li>
      <li>
       Qingdao Sculpture Museum
      </li>
      <li>
       Qingdao Etsong Natural Grass Ski Field
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Zhanshan_Temple" title="Zhanshan Temple">
        Zhanshan Temple
       </a>
       , Qingdao's oldest
       <a href="/wiki/Buddhism" title="Buddhism">
        Buddhist
       </a>
       temple.
      </li>
     </ul>

     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Other_districts_of_Qingdao">

        )
       </a>
       , located in the previous Qi State,

        Great Wall
       </a>
       of Qi

       , located 10km (6mi) to the north of
       <a href="/wiki/Laixi" title="Laixi">
        Laixi
       </a>
       City, on the middle and upperreaches of the
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dagu_River&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dagu River (page does not exist)">

       </a>

       </a>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Education">
       Education
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Education">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Post-secondary_educational_institutions">
       Post-secondary educational institutions
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Post-secondary educational institutions">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:QUST_Sifang_Campus_Main_Building.JPG">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="4608" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/QUST_Sifang_Campus_Main_Building.JPG/220px-QUST_Sifang_Campus_Main_Building.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/QUST_Sifang_Campus_Main_Building.JPG/330px-QUST_Sifang_Campus_Main_Building.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/QUST_Sifang_Campus_Main_Building.JPG/440px-QUST_Sifang_Campus_Main_Building.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:QUST_Sifang_Campus_Main_Building.JPG" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Old Main Building of Qingdao University of Science and Technology
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Qingdao is home to a large number of
      <a href="/wiki/Higher_education" title="Higher education">
       higher education
      </a>
      institutions.
      <a href="/wiki/Ocean_University_of_China" title="Ocean University of China">
       Ocean University of China
      </a>
      , formerly called Ocean University of Qingdao, is the most important university of maritime sciences in China. In addition, the
      <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_University" title="Qingdao University">
       Qingdao University
      </a>
      , the
      <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_University_of_Science_and_Technology" title="Qingdao University of Science and Technology">
       Qingdao University of Science and Technology
      </a>
      as well as the
      <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_Technological_University" title="Qingdao Technological University">
       Qingdao Technological University
      </a>
      have also been integral parts of higher education in Qingdao for decades. Other institutions include:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/China_University_of_Petroleum_(Huadong)" title="China University of Petroleum (Huadong)">
        China University of Petroleum
       </a>
       , completed its relocation from
       <a href="/wiki/Dongying" title="Dongying">
        Dongying
       </a>
       to Qingdao in 2012
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Shandong_University_of_Science_and_Technology" title="Shandong University of Science and Technology">
        Shandong University of Science and Technology
       </a>
       , main campus is based in Qingdao since 2003
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_Agricultural_University" title="Qingdao Agricultural University">
        Qingdao Agricultural University
       </a>
       , main campus is based in Qingdao since 2007
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_Technical_College" title="Qingdao Technical College">
        Qingdao Technical College
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_Binhai_University" title="Qingdao Binhai University">
        Qingdao Binhai University
       </a>
       , located at Huangdao.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <p>
      <a href="/wiki/Shandong_University" title="Shandong University">
       Shandong University
      </a>
      was located in Qingdao from 1909 to 1936. A new branch campus of the university is under construction in Jimo.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="International_schools">
       International schools
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: International schools">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       Korean International School of Qingdao
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Qingdao_MTI_International_School" title="Qingdao MTI International School">
        Qingdao MTI International School
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.qingdaoamerasia.org/" rel="nofollow">
        Qingdao Amerasia International School
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.qiss.org.cn/" rel="nofollow">
        Qingdao No.1 International School
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.qdoic.com/en/" rel="nofollow">
        Qingdao Oxford International College
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.ycef.com/" rel="nofollow">
        Yew Chung International School of Qingdao
       </a>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">
       Sports
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Sports">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Qingdao has long been a hub of professional sports in The People's Republic of China.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Stadiums">
       Stadiums
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Stadiums">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Guoxin_Gymnasium" title="Guoxin Gymnasium">
        Guoxin Gymnasium
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Hongcheng_Stadium" title="Hongcheng Stadium">
        Hongcheng Stadium
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_Tiantai_Stadium" title="Qingdao Tiantai Stadium">
        Qingdao Tiantai Stadium
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Yizhong_Sports_Center" title="Yizhong Sports Center">
        Yizhong Sports Center
       </a>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Olympic_Games">
       Olympic Games
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Olympic Games">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      Along with Beijing's hosting of the
      <a href="/wiki/2008_Summer_Olympics" title="2008 Summer Olympics">
       2008 Summer Olympics
      </a>
      , Qingdao was the host city for the Olympic Sailing competitions which took place along the shoreline by the city. These events were hosted at the
      <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_International_Sailing_Centre" title="Qingdao International Sailing Centre">
       Qingdao International Sailing Centre
      </a>
      and held in
      <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Fushan_Bay&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Fushan Bay (page does not exist)">
       Fushan Bay
      </a>
      , near the city's central business district. A hotel and an international broadcasting centre were built.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Football">
       Football
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Football">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      <a href="/wiki/Qingdao_Jonoon_F.C." title="Qingdao Jonoon F.C.">
       Qingdao Jonoon F.C.
      </a>
      (previously named Qingdao Hainiu Football Club) was founded in 1993. It is one of the founding members of the second-division of Chinese professional football league. They got the championship in their first season in 1994 and were promoted to the
      <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Jia-A_League" title="Chinese Jia-A League">
       Chinese Jia-A League
      </a>
      . In 1995, they finished 11th (out of a total 12 teams) and were relegated from the top league. Only one year later, after finishing as runner-up in the second-division, they returned to the top league. They have been part of
      <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Super_League" title="Chinese Super League">
       Chinese Super League
      </a>
      from its inauguration in 2004.
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Motorsport">
       Motorsport
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Motorsport">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      The
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/IZOD_IndyCar_Series" title="IZOD IndyCar Series">
       IZOD IndyCar Series
      </a>
      has signed a contract with the Qingdao city council to hold an
      <a href="/wiki/IndyCar" title="IndyCar">
       IndyCar
      </a>
      race in Qingdao in 2012. The race was supposed to take place on a 6.23km (3.87mi) street circuit
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">
       <a href="#cite_note-43">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        43
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      but it has been cancelled.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">
       <a href="#cite_note-44">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        44
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Surfing">
       Surfing
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Qingdao&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Surfing">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      Qingdao is one of the few cities in northern China where surfing is possible. The best surfing season is during the typhoon season (JuneOctober). The south oriented beaches of Qingdao are the most appropriate to receive swells. Shinan and Laoshan districts are reported to have the best wave and wind orientation.
     </p>

               <tr style="height:2px">
                <td colspan="2">
                </td>
               </tr>
               <tr>
                <td class="navbox-list navbox-odd" colspan="2" style="width:100%;padding:0px">
                 <div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
                  * Indicates this city has already occurred above.
                  <br/>
                  <p>
                   <sup>
                    a
                   </sup>
                   <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Direct-controlled_municipality_of_China" title="Direct-controlled municipality of China">
                    Direct-controlled Municipalities
                   </a>
                   .
                   <sup>
                    b
                   </sup>
                   <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sub-provincial_city_in_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Sub-provincial city in the People's Republic of China">
                    Sub-provincial cities as provincial capitals
                   </a>
                   .
                   <sup>
                    c
                   </sup>
                   <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sub-provincial_city_in_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Sub-provincial city in the People's Republic of China">
                    Separate state-planning cities
                   </a>
                   .
                   <sup>
                    1
                   </sup>
                   <a href="/wiki/Special_Economic_Zones_of_China" title="Special Economic Zones of China">
                    Special Economic Zone Cities
                   </a>
                   .
                   <sup>
                    2
                   </sup>
                   <a href="/wiki/Special_Economic_Zones_of_China" title="Special Economic Zones of China">
                    Coastal development cities
                   </a>
                   .
                   <br/>
                   <sup>
                    3
                   </sup>
                   Prefecture capital status established by Heilongjiang Province and not recognized by Ministry of Civil Affairs. Disputed by
                   <a href="/wiki/Oroqen_Autonomous_Banner" title="Oroqen Autonomous Banner">
                    Oroqen Autonomous Banner
                   </a>
                   , Hulunbir, Inner Mongolia as part of it.
                   <br/>
                   <sup>
                    4
                   </sup>
                   Only administers islands and waters in South China Sea and have no urban core comparable to typical cities in China.
                   <br/>
                   <sup>
                    5
                   </sup>
                   The claimed province of
                   <a href="/wiki/Taiwan_Province,_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Taiwan Province, People's Republic of China">
                    Taiwan
                   </a>
                   no longer have any internal division announced by Ministry of Civil Affairs of PRC, due to lack of actual jurisdiction. See
                   <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Template:Administrative_divisions_of_the_Republic_of_China" title="Template:Administrative divisions of the Republic of China">
                    Template:Administrative divisions of the Republic of China
                   </a>
                   instead.
                   <br/>
                  </p>
                  All provincial capitals are listed first in prefecture-level cities by province.
                 </div>
                </td>
